[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mBased on the comprehensive code analysis, I have identified a **critical OS Command[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```java[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### [0m[1;36m6[0m[39m. Explanation of Fix Strategy[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Why Simple Deletion Is Sufficient:**[0m                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe malicious code at lines [0m[1;36m398[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m400[0m[39m is:[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Self-contained [0m[1;39m([0m[39mno dependencies on or from other code[0m[1;39m)[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Not called by any other methods[0m                                                   [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Code Flow After Fix:**[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. Parse GZIP magic bytes [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m348[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m356[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ✓[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Read compression method [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m361[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m364[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m ✓[0m                                        [2m                [0m
